<!-- Keywords: spec-kit, speckit, documentation-workflow, spec-folder, template-enforcement, context-preservation, progressive-documentation, validation, spec-kit-memory, vector-search, hybrid-search, bm25, rrf-fusion, fsrs-decay, constitutional-tier, checkpoint, importance-tiers, cognitive-memory, co-activation, tiered-injection -->

# Spec Kit - Mandatory Conversation Documentation

Orchestrates mandatory spec folder creation for all conversations involving file modifications. Ensures proper documentation level selection (1-3+), template usage, and context preservation through AGENTS.md-enforced workflows.


<!-- ANCHOR:when-to-use -->
## 1. WHEN TO USE

### What is a Spec Folder?

A **spec folder** is a numbered directory (e.g., `007-auth-feature/`) that contains documentation for a single feature/task or a coordinated packet of related phase work:

Spec folders may also be nested as coordination-root packets with direct-child phase folders (e.g., `specs/02--track/022-feature/011-phase/002-child/`).

- **Purpose**: Track specifications, plans, tasks, and decisions for one unit of work
- **Location**: Under `specs/` using either `###-short-name/` at the root or nested packet paths for phased coordination
- **Contents**: Markdown files (spec.md, plan.md, tasks.md, and implementation-summary.md when work is complete) plus optional support folders such as `scratch/`, `research/`, or `review/`

Think of it as a "project folder" for AI-assisted development - it keeps context organized and enables session continuity.

### Activation Triggers

**MANDATORY for ALL file modifications:**
- Code files: JS, TS, Python, CSS, HTML
- Documentation: Markdown, README, guides
- Configuration: JSON, YAML, TOML, env templates
- Templates, knowledge base, build/tooling files

**Request patterns that trigger activation:**
- "Add/implement/create [feature]"
- "Fix/update/refactor [code]"
- "Modify/change [configuration]"
- Any keyword: add, implement, fix, update, create, modify, rename, delete, configure, analyze, phase

**Example triggers:**
- "Add email validation to the signup form" → Level 1-2
- "Refactor the authentication module" → Level 2-3
- "Fix the button alignment bug" → Level 1
- "Implement user dashboard with analytics" → Level 3

### When NOT to Use

- Pure exploration/reading (no file modifications)
- Single typo fixes (<5 characters in one file)
- Whitespace-only changes
- Auto-generated file updates (package-lock.json)
- User explicitly selects Option D (skip documentation)

**Rule of thumb:** If modifying ANY file content → Activate this skill.
Status: ✅ This requirement applies immediately once file edits are requested.

### Distributed Governance Rule

Any agent writing authored spec folder docs (`spec.md`, `plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `implementation-summary.md`, `decision-record.md`, `handover.md`, `review-report.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `resource-map.md` (optional)) MUST use templates from .opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/level_N/ for level-owned docs and the root cross-cutting templates where applicable, run `bash .opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh [spec_folder] --strict` after each file write, and route continuity updates through /memory:save. Deep-research workflow-owned packet markdown (`research/iterations/*.md`, `research/deep-research-*.md`, and progressive `research/research.md` loop updates) is exempt from that generic per-write rule; `/spec_kit:deep-research` must instead run targeted strict validation after every `spec.md` mutation it performs. @deep-research retains exclusive write access for `research/research.md`; @debug retains exclusive write access for `debug-delegation.md`.

- `handover.md` stays in the canonical recovery ladder and is maintained through `/memory:save` handover_state routing using `.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/handover.md` for initial creation.
- `review-report.md` remains owned by `@deep-review` when deep review workflows synthesize findings.
- `resource-map.md` is a peer cross-cutting template under `.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/`; it remains optional at any level and gives reviewers a lean file ledger alongside `implementation-summary.md`.

### Utility Template Triggers

| Template              | Trigger Keywords                                                                                                              | Action                    |
| --------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------- |
| `handover.md`         | "handover", "next session", "continue later", "pass context", "ending session", "save state", "multi-session", "for next AI"  | Suggest `/memory:save` handover maintenance |
| `debug-delegation.md` | "stuck", "can't fix", "tried everything", "same error", "fresh eyes", "hours on this", "still failing", "need help debugging" | Suggest Task-tool debug delegation |

**Rule:** When detected, proactively suggest the appropriate action.

## 2. SMART ROUTING

### Resource Domains

The router discovers markdown resources recursively from `references/` and `assets/` and then applies intent scoring from `RESOURCE_MAP`. Keep this section domain-focused rather than static file inventories.

- `references/memory/` for context retrieval, save workflows, trigger behavior, and indexing.
- `references/templates/` for level selection, template composition, and structure guides.
- `references/validation/` for checklist policy, verification rules, decision formats, and template compliance contracts.
- `references/structure/` for folder organization and sub-folder versioning.
- `references/workflows/` for command workflows and worked examples.
- `references/debugging/` for troubleshooting and root-cause methodology.
- `references/config/` for runtime environment configuration.

### Template and Script Sources of Truth

- Level definitions and template size guidance: [level_specifications.md](./references/templates/level_specifications.md)
- Template usage and composition rules: [template_guide.md](./references/templates/template_guide.md)
- Use `templates/level_N/` for operational templates; `core/` and `addendum/` remain composition inputs.
- Use `templates/changelog/` for packet-local nested changelog generation at completion time.
- Script architecture, build outputs, and runtime entrypoints: [scripts/README.md](./scripts/README.md)
- Memory save JSON schema and workflow contracts: [save_workflow.md](./references/memory/save_workflow.md)
- Nested packet changelog workflow: [nested_changelog.md](./references/workflows/nested_changelog.md)

Primary operational scripts:
- `spec/validate.sh`
- `spec/create.sh`
- `spec/archive.sh`
- `spec/check-completion.sh`
- `spec/recommend-level.sh`
- `templates/compose.sh`

### Resource Loading Levels

| Level       | When to Load               | Resources                    |
| ----------- | -------------------------- | ---------------------------- |

| CONDITIONAL | If intent signals match   | Intent-mapped references     |

<!-- Keywords: opencode style, script standards, mcp code quality, node code style, typescript style, ts standards, python style, py standards, bash style, shell script, json format, jsonc config, code standards opencode -->

# Code Standards - OpenCode System Code

Multi-language code standards for OpenCode system code across JavaScript, TypeScript, Python, Shell, and JSON/JSONC.

**Core Principle**: Consistency within language + Clarity across languages = maintainable system code.


## 1. WHEN TO USE

### Activation Triggers

**Use this skill when:**
- Writing or modifying OpenCode system code (.opencode/, MCP servers, scripts)
- Creating new JavaScript modules for MCP servers or utilities
- Writing Python scripts (validators, advisors, test utilities)
- Creating Shell scripts (automation, validation, deployment)
- Configuring JSON/JSONC files (manifests, schemas, configs)
- Preparing stack-specific standards evidence for `sk-code-review` baseline runs
- Need naming, formatting, or structure guidance

**Keyword triggers:**

| Language   | Keywords                                                                          |
| ---------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| JavaScript | `opencode`, `mcp`, `commonjs`, `require`, `module.exports`, `strict`              |
| TypeScript | `typescript`, `ts`, `tsx`, `interface`, `type`, `tsconfig`, `tsc`, `strict`       |
| Python     | `python`, `pytest`, `argparse`, `docstring`, `snake_case`                         |
| Shell      | `bash`, `shell`, `shebang`, `set -e`, `pipefail`                                  |
| Config     | `json`, `jsonc`, `config`, `schema`, `manifest`                                   |

### When NOT to Use

**Do NOT use this skill for:**
- Web/frontend development (use `sk-code-web` instead)
- Browser-specific patterns (DOM, observers, animations)
- CSS styling or responsive design
- CDN deployment or minification workflows
- Full development lifecycle (research/debug/verify phases)

### Skill Overview

| Aspect        | This Skill (opencode)        | sk-code-web        |
| ------------- | ---------------------------- | --------------------- |
| **Target**    | System/backend code          | Web/frontend code     |
| **Languages** | JS, TS, Python, Shell, JSON  | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |
| **Phases**    | Standards only               | 4 phases (0-3)        |
| **Browser**   | Not applicable               | Required verification |
| **Focus**     | Internal tooling             | User-facing features  |

**The Standard**: Evidence-based patterns extracted from actual OpenCode codebase files with file:line citations.

## 2. SMART ROUTING

### Resource Domains

The router discovers markdown resources recursively from `references/` and `assets/` and then applies intent scoring from `RESOURCE_MAP`. Keep this section domain-focused rather than static file inventories.

- `references/shared/` for universal cross-language patterns, structure conventions, and organization guidance.
- `references/javascript/` for JavaScript style, quality standards, and quick-reference guidance.
- `references/typescript/` for TypeScript style, quality standards, and quick-reference guidance.
- `references/python/` for Python style, quality standards, and quick-reference guidance.
- `references/shell/` for shell scripting style, quality standards, and quick-reference guidance.
- `references/config/` for JSON/JSONC style rules and configuration guidance.
- `assets/checklists/` for language-specific quality gates and completion checklists.

### Resource Loading Levels

| Level       | When to Load               | Resources                    |
| ----------- | -------------------------- | ---------------------------- |
| ALWAYS      | Every skill invocation     | Shared patterns + SKILL.md   |
| CONDITIONAL | If language keywords match | Language-specific references |
| ON_DEMAND   | Only on explicit request   | Deep-dive quality standards  |

### Smart Router Pseudocode

The authoritative routing logic for scoped loading, weighted intent scoring, and ambiguity handling.

```python
from pathlib import Path

SKILL_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
RESOURCE_BASES = (SKILL_ROOT / "references", SKILL_ROOT / "assets")
DEFAULT_RESOURCE = "references/shared/universal_patterns.md"

LANGUAGE_KEYWORDS = {
    "JAVASCRIPT": {"node": 1.8, "commonjs": 2.0, "require": 1.5, "module.exports": 2.1},
    "TYPESCRIPT": {"typescript": 2.4, "interface": 2.0, "tsconfig": 2.1, "tsc": 1.8},
    "PYTHON": {"python": 2.3, "pytest": 2.0, "argparse": 1.7, "docstring": 1.6},
    "SHELL": {"bash": 2.2, "shebang": 1.5, "set -e": 1.5, "pipefail": 1.7},
    "CONFIG": {"json": 2.0, "jsonc": 2.1, "schema": 1.8, "manifest": 1.5},
}

FILE_EXTENSIONS = {
    ".js": "JAVASCRIPT", ".mjs": "JAVASCRIPT", ".cjs": "JAVASCRIPT",
    ".ts": "TYPESCRIPT", ".tsx": "TYPESCRIPT", ".mts": "TYPESCRIPT", ".d.ts": "TYPESCRIPT",
    ".py": "PYTHON",
    ".sh": "SHELL", ".bash": "SHELL",
    ".json": "CONFIG", ".jsonc": "CONFIG"
}

NOISY_SYNONYMS = {
    "TYPESCRIPT": {"typecheck": 1.8, "lint": 1.3, "strict": 1.2, "ci": 1.0},
    "SHELL": {"shell safety": 2.0, "pipefail": 1.7, "unsafe": 1.6, "script warning": 1.4},
    "CONFIG": {"jsonc": 2.0, "schema": 1.3, "config drift": 1.4, "format": 1.2},
}

UNKNOWN_FALLBACK_CHECKLIST = [
    "List changed file extensions in the patch",
    "Confirm CI failure category (style, typecheck, shell safety, config parsing)",
    "Provide one representative failing command/output",
    "Confirm minimum verification command set before completion claim",
]

ON_DEMAND_KEYWORDS = ["gate-3-classifier", "skill_advisor.py", "vitest", "jsonl", "json schema", "commonjs helper", "mcp.json", "typescript"]

def _task_text(task) -> str:
    return " ".join([
        str(getattr(task, "context", "")),
        str(getattr(task, "query", "")),
        str(getattr(task, "path", "")),
        " ".join(getattr(task, "keywords", []) or []),
    ]).lower()

def _guard_in_skill(relative_path: str) -> str:
    resolved = (SKILL_ROOT / relative_path).resolve()
    resolved.relative_to(SKILL_ROOT)
    if resolved.suffix.lower() != ".md":
        raise ValueError(f"Only markdown resources are routable: {relative_path}")
    return resolved.relative_to(SKILL_ROOT).as_posix()

def discover_markdown_resources() -> set[str]:
    docs = []
    for base in RESOURCE_BASES:
        if base.exists():
            docs.extend(p for p in base.rglob("*.md") if p.is_file())
    return {doc.relative_to(SKILL_ROOT).as_posix() for doc in docs}

def detect_languages(task):
    """Weighted language intent scoring with top-2 ambiguity handling."""
    ext = Path(task.path).suffix.lower() if getattr(task, "path", "") else ""
    if ext in FILE_EXTENSIONS:
        return [FILE_EXTENSIONS[ext]], {FILE_EXTENSIONS[ext]: 100.0}

    text = _task_text(task)
    scores = {lang: 0.0 for lang in LANGUAGE_KEYWORDS}
    for language, signals in LANGUAGE_KEYWORDS.items():
        for term, weight in signals.items():
            if term in text:
                scores[language] += weight
    for language, synonyms in NOISY_SYNONYMS.items():
        for term, weight in synonyms.items():
            if term in text:
                scores[language] += weight

    ranked = sorted(scores.items(), key=lambda item: item[1], reverse=True)
    best_lang, best_score = ranked[0]
    second_lang, second_score = ranked[1]
    if best_score == 0:
        return ["UNKNOWN"], scores
    adaptive_limit = 3 if sum(1 for term in ["ci", "mixed", "multi", "format", "safety"] if term in text) >= 2 else 2
    if (best_score - second_score) <= 0.8:
        top_languages = [language for language, score in ranked if score > 0][:adaptive_limit]
        return top_languages, scores
    return [best_lang], scores

def route_opencode_resources(task):
    inventory = discover_markdown_resources()

.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:356:**Auto-promotion** -- memories earn their way up. After 5 positive validation marks, a normal memory promotes to important. After 10, important promotes to critical. Rate-limited to prevent bulk promotion during busy sessions.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:372:The system tracks how decisions relate to each other. Think of it like a corkboard with sticky notes connected by string. One note says "we chose JWT tokens." A string connects it to "because the session store was too slow." Another string connects that to "the Redis outage on March 5th."
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:448:**Session deduplication** -- pushes down results you already saw. If you got a result 3 turns ago, new searches rank it lower. Saves approximately 50% of tokens on follow-up queries.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:466:**Learned relevance feedback** -- watches when you mark results as useful or not. Helpful results get a boost in future queries. 10 safeguards prevent noise: denylist, rate limits, 30-day decay, per-cycle caps, minimum session thresholds, one-week trial period before boosts go live.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:494:**ANCHOR-based section retrieval** -- indexed packet docs and generated continuity artifacts can include `<!-- ANCHOR:name -->` markers. The search system indexes individual sections separately, allowing retrieval of just "decisions" or "next-steps" from a large document (~93% token savings). Files above 50K characters are always chunk-split.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:542:**Architecture:** CocoIndex (semantic, external MCP) finds code by concept. Code Graph (structural, this server) maps imports, calls and hierarchy. Memory (session, this server) preserves decisions. The compact-merger combines all three under a 4000-token budget for compaction injection. Code-graph source is self-contained under `code-graph/` with `handlers/`, `lib/`, `tools/`, and `tests/`.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:586:**Affordance evidence:** `advisor_recommend` accepts structured tool/resource hints as a sanitized affordance lane wired into the existing `derived_generated` and `graph_causal` lanes — no new scoring lane, no new `entity_kind`, no new relation type. The allowlist normalizer at `skill_advisor/lib/affordance-normalizer.ts` accepts only `skillId`/`skill_id`, `name`, `triggers[]`, `category`, and the existing relation fields (`dependsOn[]`/`depends_on[]`, `enhances[]`, `siblings[]`, `prerequisiteFor[]`/`prerequisite_for[]`, `conflictsWith[]`/`conflicts_with[]`). Free-form `description` text is intentionally ignored as a trigger source. URLs, email addresses, token-shaped fragments, control characters, and instruction-shaped strings are stripped or dropped before scoring. Sanitized triggers contribute through the existing `derived_generated` lane (`scorer/lanes/derived.ts`) with reduced weight, and normalized relations become temporary edges in the existing `graph_causal` lane (`scorer/lanes/graph-causal.ts`) reusing the existing `enhances` / `siblings` / `depends_on` / `prerequisite_for` / `conflicts_with` `EDGE_MULTIPLIER` values. Recommendation payloads cite stable `affordance:<skillId>:<index>` identifiers — never raw matched phrases. The Python graph compiler (`skill_advisor/scripts/skill_graph_compiler.py`) compiles `derived.affordances[]` into existing `signals` and sparse adjacency without changing `ALLOWED_ENTITY_KINDS` (`{"skill", "agent", "script", "config", "reference"}`).

.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:1075:Get LLM-oriented compact graph neighborhoods. Accepts CocoIndex search results as seeds for structural expansion. Modes: `neighborhood` (1-hop calls plus imports), `outline` (file symbols), `impact` (reverse callers).      2	// MODULE: Dynamic Token Budget
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	//
     5	// ADVISORY-ONLY: This module computes a token budget for a query
     6	// Based on its complexity tier, but does NOT enforce that budget
     7	// Downstream. The returned BudgetResult is handed to callers who
     8	// Are solely responsible for respecting it (e.g. by trimming
     9	// Result sets or truncating content before sending to the LLM).
    10	import { type QueryComplexityTier } from './query-classifier.js';
    11	import { isDynamicTokenBudgetEnabled } from './search-flags.js';
    12	
    13	// Feature catalog: Dynamic token budget allocation
    14	
    15	
    16	/* --- 1. TYPES & CONSTANTS --- */
    17	
    18	/** Budget (in tokens) allocated per complexity tier. */
    19	interface TokenBudgetConfig {
    20	  /** Simple query budget: 1500 tokens. */
    21	  simple: number;
    22	  /** Moderate query budget: 2500 tokens. */
    23	  moderate: number;
    24	  /** Complex query budget: 4000 tokens. */
    25	  complex: number;
    26	}
    27	
    28	/** Result of a token budget lookup. */
    29	interface BudgetResult {
    30	  /** The complexity tier that determined the budget. */
    31	  tier: QueryComplexityTier;
    32	  /** The allocated token budget. */
    33	  budget: number;
    34	  /** Whether the dynamic flag was active (false = default fallback used). */
    35	  applied: boolean;
    36	}
    37	
    38	/** Default budget when the feature flag is disabled — treat everything as complex. */
    39	const DEFAULT_BUDGET = 4000;
    40	
    41	/** Default tier-to-budget mapping when dynamic allocation is enabled.
    42	 * 1500/2500/4000 tiers balance context window cost vs. recall —
    43	 * simple queries need fewer tokens, complex queries need the full budget. */
    44	const DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG: TokenBudgetConfig = {
    45	  simple: 1500,
    46	  moderate: 2500,
    47	  complex: 4000,
    48	};
    49	
    50	/* --- 2. FEATURE FLAG --- */
    51	
    52	/* --- 3. BUDGET RESOLUTION --- */
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Get the token budget for a given query complexity tier.
    56	 *
    57	 * When SPECKIT_DYNAMIC_TOKEN_BUDGET is disabled (default), returns the DEFAULT_BUDGET
    58	 * (4000) for all queries regardless of tier, with applied=false.
    59	 *
    60	 * When enabled, maps tier to the configured budget:
    61	 *   simple   → 1500 tokens
    62	 *   moderate → 2500 tokens
    63	 *   complex  → 4000 tokens
    64	 *
    65	 * @param tier   - The complexity tier from the query classifier
    66	 * @param config - Optional custom budget config (overrides DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG)
    67	 * @returns BudgetResult with tier, budget, and applied flag
    68	 */
    69	function getDynamicTokenBudget(
    70	  tier: QueryComplexityTier,
    71	  config?: TokenBudgetConfig,
    72	): BudgetResult {
    73	  // Feature flag gate: return default when disabled
    74	  if (!isDynamicTokenBudgetEnabled()) {
    75	    return {
    76	      tier,
    77	      budget: DEFAULT_BUDGET,
    78	      applied: false,
    79	    };
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  const effectiveConfig = config ?? DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG;
    83	  const budget = effectiveConfig[tier] ?? DEFAULT_BUDGET;
    84	
    85	  return {
    86	    tier,
    87	    budget,
    88	    applied: true,
    89	  };
    90	}
    91	
    92	/* --- 4. EXPORTS --- */
    93	
    94	export {
    95	  // Types
    96	  type TokenBudgetConfig,
    97	  type BudgetResult,
    98	
    99	  // Constants
   100	  DEFAULT_BUDGET,
   101	  DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG,
   102	
   103	  // Functions
   104	  getDynamicTokenBudget,
   105	  isDynamicTokenBudgetEnabled,
   106	};

     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Stage4 Filter
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	// Final stage of the 4-stage retrieval pipeline.
     5	//
     6	// ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Stage 4 MUST NOT modify scores.
     7	// Any ordering change after Stage 3 is a bug. Score fields on
     8	// Stage4ReadonlyRow are compile-time readonly; the runtime assertion
     9	// Via captureScoreSnapshot / verifyScoreInvariant provides a second
    10	// Defence-in-depth layer.
    11	//
    12	// I/O CONTRACT:
    13	// Input:  Stage4Input { results: Stage4ReadonlyRow[], config }
    14	// Output: Stage4Output { final: Stage4ReadonlyRow[], metadata, annotations }
    15	// Key invariants:
    16	//     - No score field (similarity, score, rrfScore, intentAdjustedScore,
    17	// AttentionScore, importance_weight) may change between input and output
    18	//     - Ordering from Stage 3 is preserved for all surviving rows
    19	//     - final contains only rows at or above config.minState priority
    20	// Side effects:
    21	//     - None — this stage is read-only with respect to the database
    22	//
    23	// FILTER APPLICATION ORDER (within filterByMemoryState):
    24	// 1. memoryState priority filter — rows below minState are removed
    25	// 2. Per-tier hard limits        — STATE_LIMITS caps applied when applyStateLimits=true
    26	//
    27	// Responsibilities (in execution order):
    28	// 1. Capture score snapshot BEFORE any operations (runtime invariant)
    29	// 2. Apply memory-state filtering (filterByMemoryState)
    30	// 3. Apply evidence gap detection via TRM (Z-score confidence check)
    31	// 4. Add annotation metadata (feature flags, state stats, etc.)
    32	// 5. Verify score invariant AFTER all operations
    33	//
    34	// NOT in Stage 4: session dedup — that happens after cache in the
    35	// Main handler to avoid double-counting and cache pollution.
    36	
    37	import type { Stage4Input, Stage4Output, Stage4ReadonlyRow, PipelineRow } from './types.js';
    38	import { captureScoreSnapshot, verifyScoreInvariant, resolveEffectiveScore } from './types.js';
    39	import { isTRMEnabled, isMultiQueryEnabled } from '../search-flags.js';
    40	import { detectEvidenceGap, formatEvidenceGapWarning } from '../evidence-gap-detector.js';
    41	import { addTraceEntry } from '@spec-kit/shared/contracts/retrieval-trace';
    42	
    43	// Feature catalog: 4-stage pipeline architecture
    44	// Feature catalog: Confidence-based result truncation
    45	
    46	
    47	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    48	// 2. CONSTANTS
    49	
    50	
    51	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    52	/**
    53	 * Memory state priority map. Higher number = higher priority.
    54	 * Used to compare states numerically so filtering is O(1) per row.
    55	 */
    56	const STATE_PRIORITY: Record<string, number> = {
    57	  HOT: 5,
    58	  WARM: 4,
    59	  COLD: 3,
    60	  DORMANT: 2,
    61	  ARCHIVED: 1,
    62	};
    63	
    64	/**
    65	 * Per-tier hard limits applied when `applyStateLimits` is true.
    66	 * Prevents any single tier from monopolising the result window.
    67	 */
    68	const STATE_LIMITS: Record<string, number> = {
    69	  HOT: 50,
    70	  WARM: 30,
    71	  COLD: 20,
    72	  DORMANT: 10,
    73	  ARCHIVED: 5,
    74	};
    75	
    76	/** Fallback priority for unknown/missing memoryState values.
    77	 * Set above HOT (5) so UNKNOWN memories always pass state filters.
    78	 * memoryState column doesn't exist yet — all memories are UNKNOWN.
    79	 * Reset to 0 when the TRM state column is implemented. */
    80	const UNKNOWN_STATE_PRIORITY = 6;
    81	
    82	function normalizeStateValue(state: unknown): string | null {
    83	  if (typeof state !== 'string') {
    84	    return null;
    85	  }
    86	  const normalizedState = state.toUpperCase();
    87	  return normalizedState in STATE_PRIORITY ? normalizedState : null;
    88	}
    89	
    90	function resolveStateForFiltering(row: Stage4ReadonlyRow): string {
    91	  const explicitState = normalizeStateValue(row.memoryState);
    92	  if (explicitState) {
    93	    return explicitState;
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  return 'UNKNOWN';
    97	}
    98	
    99	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   100	// 3. TYPES
   101	
   102	
   103	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   104	/**
   105	 * Per-state tally produced by `filterByMemoryState`.
   106	 * Keys are state names (e.g. "HOT", "WARM"); values are counts.
   107	 */
   108	export type StateStats = Record<string, number>;
   109	
   110	/**
   111	 * Return value of the internal `filterByMemoryState` function.
   112	 */
   113	export interface FilterResult {
   114	  /** Rows that survived state filtering, in original order. */
   115	  filtered: Stage4ReadonlyRow[];
   116	  /** Pre-filter per-state counts (includes removed rows). */
   117	  statsBefore: StateStats;
   118	  /** Post-filter per-state counts. */
   119	  statsAfter: StateStats;
   120	  /** Total number of rows removed. */
   121	  removedCount: number;
   122	}
   123	
   124	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   125	   3. INTERNAL: filterByMemoryState
   126	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   127	
   128	/**
   129	 * Remove rows whose `memoryState` falls below `minState` priority and,
   130	 * optionally, enforce per-tier result limits via `STATE_LIMITS`.
   131	 *
   132	 * IMPORTANT: This function ONLY removes items — it never reorders or
   133	 * modifies score fields. The original ordering from Stage 3 is preserved
   134	 * for all rows that survive.
   135	 *
   136	 * @param results        - Read-only rows from Stage 3 output.
   137	 * @param minState       - Minimum acceptable state (e.g. "WARM").
   138	 * @param applyStateLimits - When true, cap each tier to STATE_LIMITS[tier].
   139	 * @returns FilterResult with the surviving rows and before/after stats.
   140	 */
   141	export function filterByMemoryState(
   142	  results: Stage4ReadonlyRow[],
   143	  minState: string,
   144	  applyStateLimits: boolean,
   145	): FilterResult {
   146	  const normalizedMinState = normalizeStateValue(minState);
   147	  const minPriority = STATE_PRIORITY[normalizedMinState ?? ''] ?? UNKNOWN_STATE_PRIORITY;
   148	
   149	  // -- 3a. Tally states before filtering --
   150	  const statsBefore: StateStats = {};
   151	  for (const row of results) {
   152	    const state = normalizeStateValue(row.memoryState) ?? 'UNKNOWN';
   153	    statsBefore[state] = (statsBefore[state] ?? 0) + 1;
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  // -- 3b. State-priority filter --
   157	  let passing = results.filter(row => {
   158	    const state = resolveStateForFiltering(row);
   159	    const priority = STATE_PRIORITY[state] ?? UNKNOWN_STATE_PRIORITY;
   160	    return priority >= minPriority;
   161	  });
   162	
   163	  // -- 3c. Per-tier limits (optional) --
   164	  if (applyStateLimits) {
   165	    const tierCounters: Record<string, number> = {};
   166	    const limitPassing: Stage4ReadonlyRow[] = [];
   167	
   168	    for (const row of passing) {
   169	      const state = resolveStateForFiltering(row);
   170	      const limit = STATE_LIMITS[state] ?? Infinity;
   171	      const count = tierCounters[state] ?? 0;
   172	
   173	      if (count < limit) {
   174	        tierCounters[state] = count + 1;
   175	        limitPassing.push(row);
   176	      }
   177	      // Rows exceeding the per-tier limit are silently dropped (no score change).
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    passing = limitPassing;
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  // -- 3d. Tally states after filtering --
   184	  const statsAfter: StateStats = {};
   185	  for (const row of passing) {
   186	    const state = resolveStateForFiltering(row);
   187	    statsAfter[state] = (statsAfter[state] ?? 0) + 1;
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  return {
   191	    filtered: passing,
   192	    statsBefore,
   193	    statsAfter,
   194	    removedCount: results.length - passing.length,
   195	  };
   196	}
   197	
   198	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   199	   4. INTERNAL: extractScoringValues
   200	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   201	
   202	/**
   203	 * Extract the best available numeric score from a row for evidence-gap
   204	 * analysis. Delegates to resolveEffectiveScore (canonical chain in types.ts)
   205	 * so scoring, sorting, and filtering all agree on precedence and normalization.
   206	 *
   207	 * A1 FIX: Previously used a different precedence order (rrfScore first) and
   208	 * did NOT divide similarity by 100, causing a 100x scale mismatch on rows
   209	 * that only had the similarity field set.
   210	 *
   211	 * @param row - A Stage4ReadonlyRow to inspect.
   212	 * @returns The best available numeric score clamped to [0,1], or 0.
   213	 */
   214	export function extractScoringValue(row: Stage4ReadonlyRow): number {
   215	  return resolveEffectiveScore(row as unknown as PipelineRow);
   216	}
   217	
   218	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   219	   5. MAIN: executeStage4
   220	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   221	
   222	/**
   223	 * Execute Stage 4 of the 4-stage retrieval pipeline: Filter + Annotate.
   224	 *
   225	 * Stage 4 is the final pipeline stage. It removes results that fall below
   226	 * the configured minimum memory state, runs the Transparent Reasoning Module
   227	 * (TRM) evidence-gap check, attaches annotation metadata, and verifies the
   228	 * score invariant before returning.
   229	 *
   230	 * **Score invariant:** No score fields are modified in Stage 4. The compile-time
   231	 * guarantee is enforced via Stage4ReadonlyRow readonly fields; the runtime check
   232	 * via captureScoreSnapshot / verifyScoreInvariant provides defence-in-depth. If
   233	 * verifyScoreInvariant throws, it indicates a Stage 4 implementation bug.
   234	 *
   235	 * **Session dedup:** Session deduplication is intentionally NOT performed here.
   236	 * It happens after the cache layer in the main handler to avoid cache pollution.
   237	 *
   238	 * @param input - Stage4Input containing read-only results and pipeline config.
   239	 * @returns Stage4Output with filtered/annotated results and metadata.
   240	 * @throws Error if verifyScoreInvariant detects any score mutation (Stage 4 bug).
   241	 */
   242	export async function executeStage4(input: Stage4Input): Promise<Stage4Output> {
   243	  const stageStart = Date.now();
   244	  const { results, config } = input;
   245	
   246	  // -- Step 1: Capture score snapshot (runtime invariant) --
   247	  //
   248	  // This snapshot is the source-of-truth for the "no score changes" assertion.
   249	  // It is taken over the FULL input set BEFORE any operations, so rows that
   250	  // Are subsequently filtered out are still in the before-snapshot. The
   251	  // VerifyScoreInvariant call skips rows not present in the after-set.
   252	  const scoresBefore = captureScoreSnapshot(results);
   253	
   254	  // -- Step 2: State filtering --
   255	  const filterResult = filterByMemoryState(
   256	    results,
   257	    config.minState,
   258	    config.applyStateLimits,
   259	  );
   260	
   261	  let workingResults: Stage4ReadonlyRow[] = filterResult.filtered;
   262	  const stateFiltered = filterResult.removedCount;
   263	
   264	  // -- Step 3: Evidence gap detection (TRM) --
   265	  let evidenceGapDetected = false;
   266	  let evidenceGapWarning: string | undefined;
   267	
   268	  if (isTRMEnabled()) {
   269	    const scores = workingResults.map(extractScoringValue);
   270	    const trm = detectEvidenceGap(scores);
   271	
   272	    evidenceGapDetected = trm.gapDetected;
   273	
   274	    if (trm.gapDetected) {
   275	      evidenceGapWarning = formatEvidenceGapWarning(trm);
   276	
   277	      // Annotate each result with the gap metadata (non-score field).
   278	      workingResults = workingResults.map(row => ({
   279	        ...row,
   280	        evidenceGap: { gapDetected: true, warning: evidenceGapWarning },
   281	      }));
   282	    }
   283	  }
   284	
   285	  // -- Step 4: Build annotation metadata --
   286	  const featureFlags: Record<string, boolean> = {
   287	    trmEnabled: isTRMEnabled(),
   288	    multiQueryEnabled: isMultiQueryEnabled(),
   289	    stateLimitsApplied: config.applyStateLimits,
   290	  };
   291	
   292	  const stateStats: Record<string, unknown> = {
   293	    minState: config.minState,
   294	    before: filterResult.statsBefore,
   295	    after: filterResult.statsAfter,
   296	    removed: stateFiltered,
   297	  };
   298	
   299	  const annotations: Stage4Output['annotations'] = {
   300	    evidenceGapWarning,
   301	    stateStats,
   302	    featureFlags,
   303	  };
   304	
   305	  // -- Step 4b: Final limit cap --
   306	  // Enforce caller's limit after all filtering to prevent degraded paths exceeding requested count
   307	  if (typeof config.limit === 'number' && config.limit > 0 && workingResults.length > config.limit) {
   308	    workingResults = workingResults.slice(0, config.limit);
   309	  }
   310	
   311	  // -- Step 5: Verify score invariant (defence-in-depth) --
   312	  //
   313	  // VerifyScoreInvariant checks every row that survived filtering.
   314	  // Rows removed by filterByMemoryState are absent from workingResults,
   315	  // So the function correctly skips them (see types.ts implementation).
   316	  // Throws [Stage4Invariant] Error if any score field was mutated.
   317	  verifyScoreInvariant(scoresBefore, workingResults);
   318	
   319	  const durationMs = Date.now() - stageStart;
   320	
   321	  // -- Trace entry --
   322	  if (config.trace) {
   323	    addTraceEntry(
   324	      config.trace,
   325	      'filter',
   326	      results.length,
   327	      workingResults.length,
   328	      durationMs,
   329	      {
   330	        stateFiltered,
   331	        evidenceGapDetected,
   332	        trmEnabled: isTRMEnabled(),
   333	        applyStateLimits: config.applyStateLimits,
   334	        minState: config.minState,
   335	      },
   336	    );
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  return {
   340	    final: workingResults,

exec

     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Skill Advisor Brief Renderer
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	
     5	import { canonicalFold } from '@spec-kit/shared/unicode-normalization';
     6	import type { AdvisorRecommendation } from './subprocess.js';
     7	
     8	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9	// 1. TYPES
    10	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    11	
    12	export interface AdvisorBriefRenderOptions {
    13	  readonly tokenCap?: number;
    14	  readonly thresholdConfig?: {
    15	    readonly confidenceThreshold?: number;
    16	    readonly uncertaintyThreshold?: number;
    17	    readonly confidenceOnly?: boolean;
    18	  };
    19	}
    20	
    21	export interface AdvisorBriefRenderableResult {
    22	  readonly status: 'ok' | 'stale' | 'skipped' | 'degraded' | 'fail_open';
    23	  readonly freshness: 'live' | 'stale' | 'absent' | 'unavailable';
    24	  readonly recommendations: readonly AdvisorRecommendation[];
    25	  readonly metrics?: {
    26	    readonly tokenCap?: number;
    27	  } | null;
    28	  readonly sharedPayload?: {
    29	    readonly metadata?: {
    30	      readonly skillLabel?: string | null;
    31	    } | null;
    32	  } | null;
    33	}
    34	
    35	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    36	// 2. CONSTANTS
    37	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    38	
    39	const DEFAULT_TOKEN_CAP = 80;
    40	const AMBIGUOUS_TOKEN_CAP = 120;
    41	const MAX_TOKEN_CAP = 120;
    42	const TOKEN_TO_CHAR_ESTIMATE = 4;
    43	const AMBIGUITY_EPSILON = 1e-9;
    44	const INSTRUCTION_LABEL_PATTERN =
    45	  /^\s*(SYSTEM|INSTRUCTION|IGNORE|EXECUTE)\s*[:=]|^\s*(<!--|```)|\b(ignore\s+(previous|all)\s+instructions|system\s*:|instruction\s*:|execute\s*:|developer\s*:|assistant\s*:)/i;
    46	const CONTROL_CHAR_PATTERN = /[\u0000-\u0008\u000B\u000C\u000E-\u001F\u007F]/g;
    47	
    48	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    49	// 3. HELPERS
    50	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    51	
    52	function clampTokenCap(tokenCap: number | undefined): number {
    53	  if (typeof tokenCap !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(tokenCap)) {
    54	    return DEFAULT_TOKEN_CAP;
    55	  }
    56	  return Math.min(Math.max(1, Math.floor(tokenCap)), MAX_TOKEN_CAP);
    57	}
    58	
    59	function capText(text: string, tokenCap: number): string {
    60	  const charCap = tokenCap * TOKEN_TO_CHAR_ESTIMATE;
    61	  if (text.length <= charCap) {
    62	    return text;
    63	  }
    64	  const truncated = text.slice(0, Math.max(1, charCap - 3)).trimEnd();
    65	  return `${truncated}...`;
    66	}
    67	
    68	function sanitizeSkillLabel(skillLabel: string | null | undefined): string | null {
    69	  if (typeof skillLabel !== 'string') {
    70	    return null;
    71	  }
    72	  const folded = canonicalFold(skillLabel);
    73	  if (/[\n\r]/.test(folded)) {
    74	    return null;
    75	  }
    76	  const singleLine = folded
    77	    .replace(CONTROL_CHAR_PATTERN, '')
    78	    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
    79	    .trim();
    80	  if (!singleLine || INSTRUCTION_LABEL_PATTERN.test(singleLine)) {
    81	    return null;
    82	  }
    83	  return singleLine;
    84	}
    85	
    86	function formatScore(value: number): string {
    87	  return Number.isFinite(value) ? value.toFixed(2) : '0.00';
    88	}
    89	
    90	function isAmbiguous(recommendations: readonly AdvisorRecommendation[]): boolean {
    91	  const [first, second] = recommendations;
    92	  return !!first && !!second && Math.abs(first.confidence - second.confidence) <= 0.05 + AMBIGUITY_EPSILON;
    93	}
    94	
    95	function metadataSkillLabel(result: AdvisorBriefRenderableResult): string | null {
    96	  const metadata = result.sharedPayload?.metadata;
    97	  return typeof metadata?.skillLabel === 'string' ? metadata.skillLabel : null;
    98	}
    99	
   100	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   101	// 4. CORE LOGIC
   102	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   103	
   104	/**
   105	 * Render the model-visible advisor brief from typed advisor output only.
   106	 *
   107	 * The renderer is the prompt-boundary guard: it ignores free-form reasons,
   108	 * descriptions, stdout/stderr, and prompt text, and emits nothing when the
   109	 * repository-authored skill label looks instruction-shaped after folding.
   110	 */
   111	export function renderAdvisorBrief(
   112	  result: AdvisorBriefRenderableResult,
   113	  options: AdvisorBriefRenderOptions = {},
   114	): string | null {
   115	  if (result.status !== 'ok') {
   116	    return null;
   117	  }
   118	  if (result.freshness !== 'live' && result.freshness !== 'stale') {
   119	    return null;
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  const tokenCap = clampTokenCap(result.metrics?.tokenCap ?? options.tokenCap);
   123	  const thresholdConfig = options.thresholdConfig;
   124	  const recommendations = result.recommendations.filter((recommendation) => (
   125	    recommendation.passes_threshold === true
   126	    || (
   127	      recommendation.confidence >= (thresholdConfig?.confidenceThreshold ?? 0.8)
   128	      && (
   129	        thresholdConfig?.confidenceOnly === true
   130	        || recommendation.uncertainty <= (thresholdConfig?.uncertaintyThreshold ?? 0.35)
   131	      )
   132	    )
   133	  ));
   134	  const [top, second] = recommendations;
   135	  if (!top) {
   136	    return null;
   137	  }
   138	
   139	  const topLabel = sanitizeSkillLabel(metadataSkillLabel(result) ?? top.skill);
   140	  if (!topLabel) {
   141	    return null;
   142	  }
   143	
   144	  if (tokenCap > DEFAULT_TOKEN_CAP && second && isAmbiguous(recommendations)) {
   145	    const secondLabel = sanitizeSkillLabel(second.skill);
   146	    if (!secondLabel) {
   147	      return null;
   148	    }
   149	    return capText(
   150	      `Advisor: ${result.freshness}; ambiguous: ${topLabel} ${formatScore(top.confidence)}/${formatScore(top.uncertainty)} vs ${secondLabel} ${formatScore(second.confidence)}/${formatScore(second.uncertainty)} pass.`,
   151	      Math.min(tokenCap, AMBIGUOUS_TOKEN_CAP),
   152	    );
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  return capText(
   156	    `Advisor: ${result.freshness}; use ${topLabel} ${formatScore(top.confidence)}/${formatScore(top.uncertainty)} pass.`,
   157	    Math.min(tokenCap, DEFAULT_TOKEN_CAP),
   158	  );
   159	}
   160	
   161	export { sanitizeSkillLabel };

   121	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

   124	   Maps each tool to its layer for quick lookup.
   125	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

   127	/**
   128	 * Defines the TOOL_LAYER_MAP constant.
   129	 */
   130	export const TOOL_LAYER_MAP: Record<string, LayerId> = {} as Record<string, LayerId>;
   131	for (const [layerId, layer] of Object.entries(LAYER_DEFINITIONS)) {
   132	  for (const tool of layer.tools) {
   133	    (TOOL_LAYER_MAP as Record<string, string>)[tool] = layerId;
   134	  }
   135	}

   137	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   138	   4. LAYER PREFIX GENERATOR
   139	
   140	   Generates description prefixes for tool descriptions.
   141	   Format: "[L#:Name] Original description..."
   142	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   143	
   144	/**
   145	 * Get the layer ID for a tool.
   146	 */
   147	export function getLayerForTool(toolName: string): LayerId | null {
   148	  return TOOL_LAYER_MAP[toolName] ?? null;
   149	}
   150	
   151	/**
   152	 * Get the layer prefix for a tool's description.
   153	 * CHK-073: Tool descriptions include layer prefix.
   154	 */
   155	export function getLayerPrefix(toolName: string): string {
   156	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   157	  if (!layerId) return '';
   158	
   159	  const layer = LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId];
   160	  return `[${layerId}:${layer.name}]`;
   161	}
   162	
   163	/**
   164	 * Enhance a tool description with layer information.
   165	 * CHK-073: Adds layer prefix to description.
   166	 */
   167	export function enhanceDescription(toolName: string, description: string): string {
   168	  const prefix = getLayerPrefix(toolName);
   169	  if (!prefix) return description;
   170	
   171	  return `${prefix} ${description}`;
   172	}

   179	
   180	/**
   181	 * Get the token budget for a tool.
   182	 */
   183	export function getLayerTokenBudget(toolName: string): number {
   184	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   185	  if (!layerId) return 1000; // Default budget
   186	
   187	  return LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId].tokenBudget;
   188	}
   189

   191	 * Get the token budget for a tool.
   192	 */
   193	export function getTokenBudget(toolName: string): number {
   194	  return getLayerTokenBudget(toolName);
   195	}
   196	
   197	/**
   198	 * Get layer information for a tool.
   199	 */
   200	export function getLayerInfo(toolName: string): LayerDefinition | null {
   201	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   202	  if (!layerId) return null;
   203	
   204	  return { ...LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId] };
   205	}

   209	 */
   210	export function getLayersByPriority(): LayerDefinition[] {
   211	  return Object.values(LAYER_DEFINITIONS).sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
   212	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Confidence Truncation
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	// Feature catalog: Confidence-based result truncation
     5	import { isConfidenceTruncationEnabled } from './search-flags.js';
     6	
     7	/* --- 1. TYPES & CONSTANTS --- */
     8	
     9	/** Generic scored result for truncation — supports both numeric and string IDs. */
    10	interface ScoredResult {
    11	  id: number | string;
    12	  score: number;
    13	  [key: string]: unknown;
    14	}
    15	
    16	/** Result of a truncation operation with full audit metadata. */
    17	interface TruncationResult {
    18	  results: ScoredResult[];
    19	  truncated: boolean;
    20	  originalCount: number;
    21	  truncatedCount: number;
    22	  /** Inclusive index of the last kept result (0-based). */
    23	  cutoffIndex: number;
    24	  medianGap: number;
    25	  cutoffGap: number;
    26	}
    27	
    28	/** Options for truncation behaviour. */
    29	interface TruncationOptions {
    30	  /** Minimum number of results to always return, regardless of gap. Default: 3. */
    31	  minResults?: number;
    32	}
    33	
    34	/** Default minimum result count. */
    35	const DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS = 3;
    36	
    37	/** Gap multiplier: gap must exceed this multiple of the median gap to trigger truncation.
    38	 * 2x median is the elbow heuristic — a gap twice the typical spread signals a relevance cliff. */
    39	const GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER = 2;
    40	
    41	/* --- 2. GAP ANALYSIS HELPERS --- */
    42	
    43	/**
    44	 * Compute consecutive score gaps for a sorted (descending) score array.
    45	 * gap[i] = scores[i] - scores[i+1]   for i in [0, n-2]
    46	 * NaN and Infinity scores are filtered out before gap computation.
    47	 * Returns empty array when fewer than 2 finite scores.
    48	 *
    49	 * @param scores - Descending-sorted array of raw scores.
    50	 * @returns Array of consecutive score gaps (length = scores.length - 1).
    51	 */
    52	function computeGaps(scores: number[]): number[] {
    53	  // NaN/Infinity from upstream bugs would corrupt gap statistics — filter them first
    54	  const finite = scores.filter(s => Number.isFinite(s));
    55	  if (finite.length < 2) return [];
    56	  const gaps: number[] = [];
    57	  for (let i = 0; i < finite.length - 1; i++) {
    58	    gaps.push(finite[i] - finite[i + 1]);
    59	  }
    60	  return gaps;
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Compute the median of an array of numbers.
    65	 * Returns 0 for an empty array.
    66	 *
    67	 * @param values - Array of numeric values.
    68	 * @returns Median value, or 0 for empty input.
    69	 */
    70	function computeMedian(values: number[]): number {
    71	  if (values.length === 0) return 0;
    72	  const sorted = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    73	  const mid = Math.floor(sorted.length / 2);
    74	  if (sorted.length % 2 === 1) {
    75	    return sorted[mid];
    76	  }
    77	  return (sorted[mid - 1] + sorted[mid]) / 2;
    78	}
    79	
    80	/* --- 3. CORE TRUNCATION LOGIC --- */
    81	
    82	/**
    83	 * Truncate results based on confidence gap analysis.
    84	 *
    85	 * Algorithm:
    86	 * 1. If fewer than minResults results, return unchanged.
    87	 * 2. Compute consecutive score gaps.
    88	 * 3. Compute median gap.
    89	 * 4. Find first index >= (minResults - 1) where gap > 2 * medianGap.
    90	 * 5. Truncate at that index + 1 (keep results 0..cutoffIndex inclusive).
    91	 * 6. If no threshold-exceeding gap found, return all results unchanged.
    92	 *
    93	 * When SPECKIT_CONFIDENCE_TRUNCATION is disabled, passes results through unchanged.
    94	 *
    95	 * Results are expected to be pre-sorted by score descending. This function
    96	 * does NOT sort; it operates on the input order.
    97	 *
    98	 * @param results - Array of scored results (expected descending by score).
    99	 * @param options - Optional truncation options (minResults).
   100	 * @returns TruncationResult with the (possibly shortened) result array and audit metadata.
   101	 */
   102	function truncateByConfidence(
   103	  results: ScoredResult[],
   104	  options?: TruncationOptions,
   105	): TruncationResult {
   106	  const minResults = options?.minResults ?? DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS;
   107	
   108	  // Defensive: filter out results with NaN/Infinity scores
   109	  const validResults = results.filter(r => Number.isFinite(r.score));
   110	
   111	  // Defensive: sort descending by score. Callers should pre-sort for efficiency.
   112	  validResults.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
   113	
   114	  const originalCount = validResults.length;
   115	
   116	  // Feature flag gate: pass through when disabled
   117	  if (!isConfidenceTruncationEnabled()) {
   118	    return {
   119	      results: [...validResults],
   120	      truncated: false,
   121	      originalCount,
   122	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   123	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   124	      medianGap: 0,
   125	      cutoffGap: 0,
   126	    };
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  // Not enough results to truncate
   130	  if (validResults.length <= minResults) {
   131	    return {
   132	      results: [...validResults],
   133	      truncated: false,
   134	      originalCount,
   135	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   136	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   137	      medianGap: 0,
   138	      cutoffGap: 0,
   139	    };
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  const scores = validResults.map(r => r.score);
   143	  const gaps = computeGaps(scores);
   144	  const medianGap = computeMedian(gaps);
   145	  const threshold = GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER * medianGap;
   146	
   147	  // When medianGap is 0 (all same scores), no meaningful gap exists — return all
   148	  if (medianGap === 0) {
   149	    return {
   150	      results: [...validResults],
   151	      truncated: false,
   152	      originalCount,
   153	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   154	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   155	      medianGap: 0,
   156	      cutoffGap: 0,
   157	    };
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  // Search for the first gap that exceeds the threshold, starting from minResults - 1.
   161	  // Gap[i] is the gap between result i and result i+1.
   162	  // If gap[i] > threshold, we keep results 0..i (cutoffIndex = i).
   163	  let cutoffIndex = -1;
   164	  let cutoffGap = 0;
   165	
   166	  for (let i = minResults - 1; i < gaps.length; i++) {
   167	    if (gaps[i] > threshold) {
   168	      cutoffIndex = i;
   169	      cutoffGap = gaps[i];
   170	      break;
   171	    }
   172	  }
   173	
   174	  // No significant gap found — return all results
   175	  if (cutoffIndex === -1) {
   176	    return {
   177	      results: [...validResults],
   178	      truncated: false,
   179	      originalCount,
   180	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   181	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   182	      medianGap,
   183	      cutoffGap: 0,
   184	    };
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  // Truncate: keep validResults[0..cutoffIndex] inclusive
   188	  const truncatedResults = validResults.slice(0, cutoffIndex + 1);
   189	
   190	  return {
   191	    results: truncatedResults,
   192	    truncated: true,
   193	    originalCount,
   194	    truncatedCount: truncatedResults.length,
   195	    cutoffIndex,
   196	    medianGap,
   197	    cutoffGap,
   198	  };
   199	}
   200	
   201	/* --- 5. EXPORTS --- */
   202	
   203	export {
   204	  // Types
   205	  type ScoredResult,
   206	  type TruncationResult,
   207	  type TruncationOptions,
   208	
   209	  // Constants
   210	  DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS,
   211	  GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER,
   212	
   213	  // Functions
   214	  truncateByConfidence,
   215	  isConfidenceTruncationEnabled,
   216	
   217	  // Internal helpers (exported for testing)
   218	  computeGaps,
   219	  computeMedian,
   220	};

  2280	/**
  2281	 * Estimate token count for a text string using a chars/4 heuristic.
  2282	 * @param text - The text to estimate tokens for.
  2283	 * @returns Approximate token count (ceiling of length / 4).
  2284	 */
  2285	function estimateTokenCount(text: string): number {
  2286	  if (!text) return 0;
  2287	  return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
  2288	}

  2290	function estimateStructuredValueChars(value: unknown, seen: WeakSet<object>): number {
  2291	  if (value == null) return 4;
  2292	
  2293	  if (typeof value === 'string') return value.length + 2;
  2294	  if (typeof value === 'number' || typeof value === 'bigint') return String(value).length;
  2295	  if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value ? 4 : 5;
  2296	
  2297	  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
  2298	    let chars = 2;
  2299	    for (const item of value) {
  2300	      chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(item, seen) + 1;
  2301	    }
  2302	    return chars;
  2303	  }
  2304	
  2305	  if (typeof value !== 'object') return 0;
  2306	  if (seen.has(value)) return 8;
  2307	  seen.add(value);
  2308	
  2309	  let chars = 2;
  2310	  for (const [key, nestedValue] of Object.entries(value as Record<string, unknown>)) {
  2311	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2312	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(nestedValue, seen) + 1;
  2313	  }
  2314	  return chars;
  2315	}

  2317	/**
  2318	 * Estimate the token footprint of a single HybridSearchResult.
  2319	 * @param result - The search result to measure.
  2320	 * @returns Approximate token count based on serialized key-value lengths.
  2321	 */
  2322	function estimateResultTokens(result: HybridSearchResult): number {
  2323	  const record = result as Record<string, unknown>;
  2324	  const seen = new WeakSet<object>();
  2325	  const handledKeys = new Set([
  2326	    'id',
  2327	    'score',
  2328	    'source',
  2329	    'title',
  2330	    'content',
  2331	    'sources',
  2332	    'spec_folder',
  2333	    'file_path',
  2334	    'traceMetadata',
  2335	    'parentMemoryId',
  2336	    'chunkIndex',
  2337	    'similarity',
  2338	    'combined_lexical_score',
  2339	  ]);
  2340	
  2341	  let chars = 0;
  2342	  for (const key of handledKeys) {
  2343	    if (!(key in record)) continue;
  2344	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2345	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(record[key], seen) + 1;
  2346	  }
  2347	
  2348	  for (const key of Object.keys(record)) {
  2349	    if (handledKeys.has(key)) continue;
  2350	    const value = record[key];
  2351	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2352	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(value, seen) + 1;
  2353	  }
  2354	
  2355	  return Math.ceil(chars / 4);
  2356	}

  2416	    if (cached !== undefined) {
  2417	      return cached;
  2418	    }
  2419	
  2420	    const estimate = estimateResultTokens(result);
  2421	    tokenEstimateCache.set(cacheKey, estimate);
  2422	    return estimate;
  2423	  };
  2424	
  2425	  const totalTokens = sorted.reduce((sum, result) => sum + getTokenEstimate(result), 0);
  2426	
  2427	  if (totalTokens <= effectiveBudget) {
  2428	    return { results: sorted, truncated: false };
  2429	  }
  2430	
  2431	  // Single-result overflow: summarize when content is included, otherwise keep
  2432	  // the lone result and mark the overflow for callers.
  2433	  if (sorted.length === 1) {
  2434	    const outputResult = includeContent
  2435	      ? createSummaryFallback(sorted[0]!, effectiveBudget)
  2436	      : sorted[0]!;
  2437	    const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2438	      queryId,
  2439	      candidateCount: 1,
  2440	      totalTokens,
  2441	      budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2442	      truncatedToCount: 1,
  2443	      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2444	    };
  2445	    console.warn(
  2446	      `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow (single-result fallback): ` +
  2447	      `${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget`
  2448	    );
  2449	    return { results: [outputResult], truncated: true, overflow };
  2450	  }
  2451	
  2452	  // Greedy accumulation: take highest-scoring results until budget exhausted
  2453	  const accepted: HybridSearchResult[] = [];
  2454	  let accumulated = 0;
  2455	
  2456	  for (const result of sorted) {
  2457	    const tokens = getTokenEstimate(result);
  2458	    if (accumulated + tokens > effectiveBudget) {
  2459	      if (accepted.length > 0) {
  2460	        break;
  2461	      }
  2462	      continue;
  2463	    }
  2464	    accepted.push(result);
  2465	    accumulated += tokens;
  2466	    if (accumulated >= effectiveBudget) break;
  2467	  }
  2468	
  2469	  if (accepted.length === 0 && sorted.length > 0) {
  2470	    const outputResult = includeContent
  2471	      ? createSummaryFallback(sorted[0]!, effectiveBudget)
  2472	      : sorted[0]!;
  2473	    const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2474	      queryId,
  2475	      candidateCount: results.length,
  2476	      totalTokens,
  2477	      budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2478	      truncatedToCount: 1,
  2479	      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2480	    };
  2481	
  2482	    console.warn(
  2483	      `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow (top-result fallback): ` +
  2484	      `${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget`
  2485	    );
  2486	
  2487	    return { results: [outputResult], truncated: true, overflow };
  2488	  }
  2489	
  2490	  const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2491	    queryId,
  2492	    candidateCount: results.length,
  2493	    totalTokens,
  2494	    budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2495	    truncatedToCount: accepted.length,
  2496	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2497	  };
  2498	
  2499	  console.warn(
  2500	    `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow: ${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget, ` +
  2501	    `truncated ${results.length} → ${accepted.length} results`
  2502	  );
  2503	
  2504	  return { results: accepted, truncated: true, overflow };
  2505	}

   263	function extractBlockers(results: SearchResultEntry[]): string[] {
   264	  const blockers: string[] = [];
   265	
   266	  const lowConfidence = results.filter(r => r.confidence?.label === 'low');
   267	  if (lowConfidence.length > 0) {
   268	    blockers.push(`${lowConfidence.length} result(s) have low confidence scores`);
   269	  }
   270	
   271	  const archivedOrCold = results.filter(
   272	    r => r.memoryState === 'COLD' || r.memoryState === 'ARCHIVED'
   273	  );
   274	  if (archivedOrCold.length > 0) {
   275	    blockers.push(`${archivedOrCold.length} result(s) are cold/archived — may be stale`);
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  return blockers;
   279	}

   281	function computeTokenStats(text: string, resultCount: number) {

   283	  return {
   284	    totalTokens,
   285	    resultCount,

   296	// ── Profile formatters ─────────────────────────────────────────
   297	
   298	/**
   299	 * Format results as the `quick` profile.
   300	 * Returns only the top result with a one-line explanation and an
   301	 * omitted count. Maximises token reduction.
   302	 */
   303	function formatQuick(input: ProfileFormatterInput): QuickProfile {
   304	  const { results } = input;
   305	  const originalText = JSON.stringify(input);
   306	  const originalTokens = estimateTokens(originalText);
   307	
   308	  if (results.length === 0) {
   309	    return {
   310	      topResult: null,
   311	      oneLineWhy: 'No results found',
   312	      omittedCount: 0,
   313	      tokenReduction: {
   314	        originalTokens,
   315	        returnedTokens: estimateTokens('{}'),
   316	        savingsPercent: 99,
   317	      },
   318	    };
   319	  }
   320	
   321	  const topResult = results[0];
   322	  const oneLineWhy = getOneLineWhy(topResult, 0);
   323	  const omittedCount = results.length - 1;
   324	
   325	  const quickPayload = { topResult, oneLineWhy, omittedCount };
   326	  const returnedTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(quickPayload));
   327	  const savingsPercent = originalTokens > 0
   328	    ? Math.round(((originalTokens - returnedTokens) / originalTokens) * 100)
   329	    : 0;
   330	
   331	  return {
   332	    topResult,
   333	    oneLineWhy,
   334	    omittedCount,
   335	    tokenReduction: {
   336	      originalTokens,
   337	      returnedTokens,
   338	      savingsPercent: Math.max(0, savingsPercent),
   339	    },
   340	  };
   341	}

   629	    const lastResult = currentResults[lastIndex];
   630	    if (!lastResult || typeof lastResult !== 'object') {
   631	      return null;
   632	    }
   633	
   634	    for (const key of truncateKeys) {
   635	      const originalValue = lastResult[key];
   636	      if (typeof originalValue !== 'string' || originalValue.length === 0) {
   637	        continue;
   638	      }
   639	
   640	      let bestResult: ContextResult | null = null;
   641	      let bestTokens = Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
   642	      let low = 0;
   643	      let high = originalValue.length;
   644	
   645	      while (low <= high) {
   646	        const mid = Math.floor((low + high) / 2);
   647	        const candidateResults = [...currentResults];
   648	        candidateResults[lastIndex] = {
   649	          ...lastResult,
   650	          [key]: originalValue.slice(0, mid),
   651	        };
   652	
   653	        innerEnvelope.data = {
   654	          ...((innerEnvelope.data as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {}),
   655	          results: candidateResults,
   656	          count: candidateResults.length,
   657	        };
   658	
   659	        const candidateContent = contentEntries.map((entry, index) => (
   660	          index === 0 ? { type: entry.type, text: JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope) } : { ...entry }
   661	        ));
   662	        const candidateResult = {
   663	          ...truncatedResult,
   664	          content: candidateContent,
   665	        } as ContextResult;
   666	        const candidateTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(candidateResult));
   667	
   668	        if (candidateTokens <= budgetTokens) {
   669	          bestResult = candidateResult;
   670	          bestTokens = candidateTokens;
   671	          low = mid + 1;
   672	        } else {
   673	          high = mid - 1;
   674	        }
   675	      }
   676	
   677	      if (bestResult) {
   678	        return {
   679	          result: bestResult,
   680	          actualTokens: bestTokens,
   681	        };
   682	      }
   683	    }
   684	
   685	    return null;
   686	  };
   687	
   688	  // Try to find and truncate the inner results array
   689	  const contentArr = (truncatedResult as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<{ type: string; text: string }> | undefined;
   690	  let parseFailedInnerText: string | undefined;
   691	  // REQ-002 (Cluster 1): Track survivors so the fallback path can preserve them
   692	  // instead of zero-filling.
   693	  let preservedAfterStructural: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = [];
   694	  if (contentArr && Array.isArray(contentArr) && contentArr.length > 0 && contentArr[0]?.text) {
   695	    try {
   696	      const innerEnvelope = JSON.parse(contentArr[0].text);
   697	      const innerResults = innerEnvelope?.data?.results;
   698	
   699	      if (Array.isArray(innerResults) && innerResults.length > 0) {
   700	        originalResultCount = innerResults.length;
   701	
   702	        // Results should already be sorted by score (highest first)
   703	        // Remove items from the end until we fit within budget
   704	        const currentResults = [...innerResults];
   705	        let currentTokens = actualTokens;
   706	
   707	        // Phase 1: Adaptive content truncation — truncate content fields before dropping results
   708	        const MAX_CONTENT_CHARS = 500;
   709	        for (const r of currentResults) {
   710	          if (r.content && typeof r.content === 'string' && r.content.length > MAX_CONTENT_CHARS) {
   711	            r.content = r.content.substring(0, MAX_CONTENT_CHARS) + '...';
   712	            r.contentTruncated = true;
   713	          }
   714	        }
   715	        // Re-estimate after content truncation
   716	        innerEnvelope.data.results = currentResults;
   717	        innerEnvelope.data.count = currentResults.length;
   718	        currentTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope));
   719	
   720	        // Phase 2: Drop lowest-scored results if still over budget
   721	        while (currentResults.length > 1 && currentTokens > budgetTokens) {
   722	          // Remove the last (lowest-scored) result
   723	          const removed = currentResults.pop();
   724	          const removedTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(removed));
   725	          currentTokens -= removedTokens;

   103	type EnvelopeRecord = Record<string, unknown> & { meta?: Record<string, unknown> };
   104	
   105	function ensureEnvelopeMeta(envelope: EnvelopeRecord): Record<string, unknown> {
   106	  const meta = envelope.meta;
   107	  if (typeof meta === 'object' && meta !== null && !Array.isArray(meta)) {
   108	    return meta;
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  const nextMeta: Record<string, unknown> = {};
   112	  envelope.meta = nextMeta;
   113	  return nextMeta;
   114	}
   115	
   116	export function syncEnvelopeTokenCount<T>(envelope: MCPEnvelope<T> | EnvelopeRecord): number {
   117	  const meta = ensureEnvelopeMeta(envelope as EnvelopeRecord);
   118	  const currentTokenCount = meta.tokenCount;
   119	  let previousCount = typeof currentTokenCount === 'number' && Number.isFinite(currentTokenCount)
   120	    ? currentTokenCount
   121	    : -1;
   122	
   123	  // Converges in 2-3 iterations; the 5-iteration cap is a safety bound.
   124	  for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 5; attempt += 1) {
   125	    const nextTokenCount = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(envelope, null, 2));
   126	    meta.tokenCount = nextTokenCount;
   127	    if (nextTokenCount === previousCount) {
   128	      return nextTokenCount;
   129	    }
   130	    previousCount = nextTokenCount;
   131	  }
   132	
   133	  return typeof meta.tokenCount === 'number' ? meta.tokenCount : 0;
   134	}
   135	
   136	export function serializeEnvelopeWithTokenCount<T>(envelope: MCPEnvelope<T> | EnvelopeRecord): string {
   137	  syncEnvelopeTokenCount(envelope);
   138	  return JSON.stringify(envelope, null, 2);
   139	}

   246	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   247	   5. AUTO-SURFACE MEMORIES
   248	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   249	
   250	function enforceAutoSurfaceTokenBudget(
   251	  result: AutoSurfaceResult | null,
   252	  tokenBudget: number,
   253	  hookName: 'tool-dispatch' | 'compaction' | 'memory-aware'
   254	): AutoSurfaceResult | null {
   255	  if (!result) {
   256	    return null;
   257	  }
   258	
   259	  const measureTokens = (candidate: AutoSurfaceResult): number =>
   260	    estimateTokenCount(JSON.stringify(candidate));
   261	
   262	  const budgetLimit = Number.isFinite(tokenBudget) && tokenBudget > 0
   263	    ? tokenBudget
   264	    : TOOL_DISPATCH_TOKEN_BUDGET;
   265	
   266	  let boundedResult: AutoSurfaceResult = result;
   267	  let tokenCount = measureTokens(boundedResult);
   268	
   269	  if (tokenCount <= budgetLimit) {
   270	    return boundedResult;
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  const triggered = [...boundedResult.triggered];
   274	  while (triggered.length > 0 && tokenCount > budgetLimit) {
   275	    triggered.pop();
   276	    boundedResult = { ...boundedResult, triggered };
   277	    tokenCount = measureTokens(boundedResult);
   278	  }
   279	
   280	  const constitutional = [...boundedResult.constitutional];
   355	  return [...triggered]
   356	    .sort((a, b) => {
   357	      const scoreA = (a.matchedPhrases.length + a.importanceWeight * 0.1) *
   358	        (attentionIds.has(a.memoryId) ? ATTENTION_BOOST_FACTOR : 1.0);
   359	      const scoreB = (b.matchedPhrases.length + b.importanceWeight * 0.1) *
   360	        (attentionIds.has(b.memoryId) ? ATTENTION_BOOST_FACTOR : 1.0);
   361	      return scoreB - scoreA;
   362	    });
   363	}
   364	
   365	async function autoSurfaceMemories(
   366	  contextHint: string,
   367	  tokenBudget: number = TOOL_DISPATCH_TOKEN_BUDGET,
   368	  hookName: 'tool-dispatch' | 'compaction' | 'memory-aware' = 'memory-aware'
   369	): Promise<AutoSurfaceResult | null> {
   370	  const startTime = Date.now();
   371	
   372	  try {
   373	    // Get constitutional memories (always surface)
   374	    const constitutional = await getConstitutionalMemories();
   375	
   376	    // Get triggered memories via fast phrase matching
   377	    let triggered = triggerMatcher.matchTriggerPhrases(contextHint, 5);
   378	
   379	    // Phase C: Attention-enriched boost — re-rank triggered results that
   380	    // also appear in the working memory active set.
   381	    try {
   382	      const attentionIds = getAttentionWeightedMemoryIds(5);
   383	      if (attentionIds.size > 0 && triggered.length > 0) {
   384	        triggered = applyAttentionBoost(triggered, attentionIds);
   385	      }
   386	    } catch (_boostErr: unknown) {
   387	      // Graceful degradation — attention boost is optional
   388	    }
   389	
   390	    const latencyMs = Date.now() - startTime;
   391	
   392	    // Only return if we have something to surface
   393	    if (constitutional.length === 0 && triggered.length === 0) {
   394	      return null;
   395	    }
   396	
   397	    // PI-A4: Enrich constitutional memories with retrieval_directive metadata.
   398	    // Pure content transformation — scoring is unchanged.
   399	    const enrichedConstitutional = enrichWithRetrievalDirectives(constitutional);
   400	
   401	    return enforceAutoSurfaceTokenBudget({
   402	      constitutional: enrichedConstitutional,
   403	      triggered: triggered.map((t: triggerMatcher.TriggerMatch) => ({
   404	        memory_id: t.memoryId,
   405	        spec_folder: t.specFolder,
   406	        title: t.title ?? 'Untitled',
   407	        matched_phrases: t.matchedPhrases,
   408	      })),
   409	      surfaced_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   410	      latencyMs: latencyMs,
   411	    }, tokenBudget, hookName);
   412	  } catch (err: unknown) {
   413	    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   414	    console.warn('[SK-004] Auto-surface failed:', message);
   415	    return null;
   416	  }
   417	}

   302	/**
   303	 * Phase C: Get top-N attention-weighted memory IDs from working memory.
   304	 * Used to boost trigger-matched results that also appear in the active
   305	 * working set, improving surface relevance.
   306	 *
   307	 * @param limit - Maximum number of memory IDs to return
   308	 * @returns Set of memory IDs with high attention in working memory
   309	 */
   310	function getAttentionWeightedMemoryIds(limit: number = 5): Set<number> {
   311	  try {
   312	    const db: Database | null = vectorIndex.getDb();
   313	    if (!db) return new Set();
   314	
   315	    // Query top attention-weighted memories, scoped to the current session
   316	    // by filtering to entries focused within the last hour. This prevents
   317	    // stale cross-session entries from influencing auto-surface ordering.
   318	    const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();
   319	    const rows = db.prepare(`
   320	      SELECT DISTINCT wm.memory_id
   321	      FROM working_memory wm
   322	      WHERE wm.memory_id IS NOT NULL
   323	        AND wm.attention_score > ?
   324	        AND wm.last_focused >= ?
   325	      ORDER BY wm.attention_score DESC, wm.last_focused DESC
   326	      LIMIT ?
   327	    `).all(workingMemory.DECAY_FLOOR, oneHourAgo, limit) as Array<{ memory_id: number }>;
   328	
   329	    return new Set(rows.map(r => r.memory_id));

    72	/**
    73	 * Enrich with code graph symbols near mentioned files.
    74	 * Dynamically imports code-graph-db to avoid hard dependency.
    75	 */
    76	async function enrichWithCodeGraphSymbols(
    77	  paths: string[],
    78	  tokenBudget: number,
    79	): Promise<string[]> {
    80	  if (paths.length === 0) return [];
    81	
    82	  try {
    83	    const graphDb = await import('../../code_graph/lib/code-graph-db.js');
    84	    const db = graphDb.getDb();
    85	    if (!db) return [];
    86	
    87	    // Look up symbols in the mentioned files (top 3 per file, max 10 total)
    88	    const symbols: string[] = [];
    89	    for (const filePath of paths.slice(0, 3)) {
    90	      const rows = db.prepare(`
    91	        SELECT name, kind FROM code_nodes
    92	        WHERE file_path LIKE ? OR file_path LIKE ?
    93	        ORDER BY kind ASC, name ASC
    94	        LIMIT 3
    95	      `).all(`%${filePath}`, `%${filePath.replace(/^\.\//, '')}`) as Array<{ name: string; kind: string }>;
    96	
    97	      for (const row of rows) {
    98	        symbols.push(`${row.kind}:${row.name}`);
    99	        if (symbols.length >= 10) break;
   100	      }
   101	      if (symbols.length >= 10) break;
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    if (symbols.length === 0) return [];
   105	
   106	    const hint = `[code-graph] Symbols near mentioned files: ${symbols.join(', ')}`;
   107	    if (estimateTokenCount(hint) > tokenBudget) {
   108	      // Trim to fit budget
   109	      const trimmed = `[code-graph] ${symbols.slice(0, 5).join(', ')}`;
   110	      return estimateTokenCount(trimmed) <= tokenBudget ? [trimmed] : [];
   111	    }
   112	    return [hint];
   113	  } catch {
   114	    // Code graph not available — non-fatal
   115	    return [];
   116	  }
   117	}

   120	 * Enrich with session continuity warning if quality is degraded.
   150	 */
   151	export async function runPassiveEnrichment(
   152	  responseText: string,
   153	  options?: EnrichmentOptions,
   154	): Promise<EnrichmentResult> {
   155	  const startTime = Date.now();
   156	  const deadlineMs = options?.deadlineMs ?? DEFAULT_DEADLINE_MS;
   157	  const tokenBudget = options?.tokenBudget ?? DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET;
   158	
   159	  // Recursion guard
   160	  if (enrichmentInProgress) {
   161	    return { hints: [], tokenCount: 0, latencyMs: 0, skipped: true, skipReason: 'recursion_guard' };
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  enrichmentInProgress = true;
   165	  try {
   166	    const hints: string[] = [];
   167	    let tokensUsed = 0;
   168	
   169	    // Step 1: Code graph symbol enrichment
   170	    if (Date.now() - startTime < deadlineMs) {
   171	      const paths = extractMentionedPaths(responseText);
   172	      const graphHints = await enrichWithCodeGraphSymbols(paths, tokenBudget - tokensUsed);
   173	      for (const hint of graphHints) {
   174	        const cost = estimateTokenCount(hint);
   175	        if (tokensUsed + cost > tokenBudget) break;
   176	        hints.push(hint);
   177	        tokensUsed += cost;
   178	      }
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    // Step 2: Session continuity warning
   182	    if (Date.now() - startTime < deadlineMs && tokensUsed < tokenBudget) {
   183	      const sessionHints = await enrichWithSessionWarning();
   184	      for (const hint of sessionHints) {
   185	        const cost = estimateTokenCount(hint);
   186	        if (tokensUsed + cost > tokenBudget) break;
   187	        hints.push(hint);
   188	        tokensUsed += cost;
   189	      }
   190	    }
