   102	/** Build context from resolved anchors using specified query mode */
   103	export function buildContext(args: ContextArgs): ContextResult {
   104	  const queryMode = args.queryMode ?? 'neighborhood';
   105	  const budgetTokens = args.budgetTokens ?? 1200;
   106	  const seeds = args.seeds ?? [];
   107	  const deadlineMs = args.deadlineMs ?? defaultDeadlineMsForProfile(args.profile);
   108	  const speckitQueryStart = isSpeckitMetricsEnabled() ? performance.now() : 0;
   109	  const speckitModeLabel = speckitQueryModeLabel(queryMode);
   110	  const resolvedAnchors = resolveSeeds(seeds);
   111	
   112	  // If no seeds but subject given, create seed from subject
   113	  if (resolvedAnchors.length === 0 && args.subject) {
   114	    const subjectRef = resolveSubjectToRef(args.subject);
   115	    if (subjectRef) resolvedAnchors.push(subjectRef);
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  // Empty seeds + no subject → outline mode fallback
   119	  if (resolvedAnchors.length === 0) {
   120	    if (isSpeckitMetricsEnabled()) {
   121	      speckitMetrics.incrementCounter('spec_kit.graph.query_cache_misses_total', { mode: speckitModeLabel });
   122	    }
   123	    return buildEmptyFallback(queryMode, budgetTokens);
   124	  }
   125	  if (isSpeckitMetricsEnabled()) {
   126	    speckitMetrics.incrementCounter('spec_kit.graph.query_cache_hits_total', { mode: speckitModeLabel });
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  const sections: GraphContextSection[] = [];
   130	  let totalNodes = 0;
   170	    if (expansion.deadlineExceeded) {
   171	      partialReasons.add('deadline');
   172	      omittedAnchors += resolvedAnchors.length - sections.length;
   173	      break;
   174	    }
   175	  }
   176	
   177	  const formattedTextBrief = formatTextBrief(sections, budgetTokens, resolvedAnchors);
   178	  if (formattedTextBrief.omittedSections > 0 || formattedTextBrief.truncated) {
   179	    partialReasons.add('budget');
   180	  }
   181	  const combinedSummary = buildCombinedSummary(resolvedAnchors, sections);
   182	  const nextActions = suggestNextActions(resolvedAnchors, sections, queryMode);
   183	  const freshness = computeFreshness();
   184	  if (isSpeckitMetricsEnabled()) {
   185	    const freshnessLabel = freshness.staleness === 'fresh' || freshness.staleness === 'recent' ? 'live' : freshness.staleness === 'stale' ? 'stale' : 'unavailable';
   186	    speckitMetrics.recordHistogram('spec_kit.graph.query_latency_ms', performance.now() - speckitQueryStart, { mode: speckitModeLabel, freshness_state: freshnessLabel });
   187	  }
   188	
   189	  return {
   190	    queryMode,
   191	    resolvedAnchors,
   192	    graphContext: sections,
   193	    textBrief: formattedTextBrief.text,
   194	    combinedSummary,
   195	    nextActions,
   196	    metadata: {
   197	      totalNodes,
   198	      totalEdges,
   199	      budgetUsed: Math.ceil(formattedTextBrief.text.length / 4),
   200	      budgetLimit: budgetTokens,
   201	      deadlineMs,
   202	      partialOutput: {
   203	        isPartial: partialReasons.size > 0,
   204	        reasons: [...partialReasons],
   205	        omittedSections: omittedSections + formattedTextBrief.omittedSections,
   520	        score: null,
   521	        snippet: null,
   522	        range: null,
   523	        provider: 'code_graph',
   524	      };
   525	    }
   526	  } catch { /* DB not available */ }
   527	  return null;
   528	}

   530	/**
   531	 * Format sections into compact text brief within token budget.
   532	 * Never-drops guarantee: always includes top seed, root anchor, one boundary edge, one next action.
   533	 */
   534	function formatTextBrief(sections: GraphContextSection[], budgetTokens: number, _anchors?: ArtifactRef[]): FormattedTextBrief {
   535	  const maxChars = budgetTokens * 4;
   536	  const lines: string[] = [];
   537	  let omittedSections = 0;
   538	
   539	  // Priority rendering: first section is always fully rendered (never dropped)
   540	  for (let i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
   541	    const section = sections[i];
   542	    const isFirst = i === 0;
   543	    const nodeLimit = isFirst ? 15 : Math.max(5, 15 - i * 3);
   544	    const edgeLimit = isFirst ? 10 : Math.max(3, 10 - i * 2);
   545	
   546	    lines.push(`### ${section.anchor}`);
   547	
   548	    if (section.nodes.length > 0) {
   549	      lines.push('Symbols:');
   550	      for (const n of section.nodes.slice(0, nodeLimit)) {
   551	        lines.push(`  ${n.kind} ${n.name} (${n.file}:${n.line})`);
   552	      }
   553	      if (section.nodes.length > nodeLimit) {
   554	        lines.push(`  ... +${section.nodes.length - nodeLimit} more`);
   555	      }
   556	    }
   557	
   558	    if (section.edges.length > 0) {
   559	      lines.push('Relationships:');
   560	      for (const e of section.edges.slice(0, edgeLimit)) {
   561	        const metadata = [
   562	          e.reason ? `reason=${e.reason}` : null,
   563	          e.step ? `step=${e.step}` : null,
   564	          typeof e.confidence === 'number' ? `confidence=${e.confidence}` : null,
   565	        ].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   566	        lines.push(`  ${e.from} -[${e.type}${metadata ? ` ${metadata}` : ''}]-> ${e.to}`);
   567	      }
   568	      if (section.edges.length > edgeLimit) {
   569	        lines.push(`  ... +${section.edges.length - edgeLimit} more`);
   570	      }
   571	    }
   572	
   573	    lines.push('');
   574	
   575	    // Budget check: stop adding sections if we're over budget (but first section always included)

     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Budget Allocator
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	// Distributes a total token budget across multiple context sources
     5	// using floor allocations + overflow redistribution.
     6	
     7	/** Per-source budget configuration */
     8	export interface SourceBudget {
     9	  name: string;
    10	  floor: number;
    11	  actualSize: number; // 0 if source is empty
    12	}
    13	
    14	/** Allocation result for a single source */
    15	export interface SourceAllocation {
    16	  name: string;
    17	  floor: number;
    18	  requested: number;
    19	  granted: number;
    20	  dropped: number;
    21	}
    22	
    23	/** Combined allocation result */
    24	export interface AllocationResult {
    25	  totalBudget: number;
    26	  totalUsed: number;
    27	  overflow: number;
    28	  allocations: SourceAllocation[];
    29	}
    30	
    31	/** Default floor layout for the 4000-token compact brief budget */
    32	export const DEFAULT_FLOORS = {
    33	  constitutional: 700,
    34	  codeGraph: 1200,
    35	  cocoIndex: 900,
    36	  triggered: 400,
    37	  overflow: 800,
    38	} as const;
    39	
    40	/** Priority order for overflow redistribution (highest first) */
    41	const PRIORITY_ORDER = ['constitutional', 'codeGraph', 'cocoIndex', 'sessionState', 'triggered'] as const;
    42	
    43	/**
    44	 * Allocate token budget across sources.
    45	 *
    46	 * Algorithm:
    47	 * 1. Assign floor to each source (capped at actual size)
    48	 * 2. Calculate overflow from empty/under-floor sources
    49	 * 3. Redistribute overflow by priority order
    50	 * 4. Enforce total budget cap with deterministic trim
    51	 */
    52	export function allocateBudget(
    53	  sources: SourceBudget[],
    54	  totalBudget: number = 4000,
    55	): AllocationResult {
    56	  const allocations: SourceAllocation[] = [];
    57	  const floorTotal = sources.reduce((sum, source) => sum + source.floor, 0);
    58	  let overflowPool = Math.max(totalBudget - floorTotal, 0);
    59	
    60	  // Step 1: Assign floors, collect overflow from empty sources
    61	  for (const source of sources) {
    62	    const floor = source.floor;
    63	    const granted = Math.min(floor, source.actualSize);
    64	    const unused = floor - granted;
    65	    overflowPool += unused;
    66	
    67	    allocations.push({
    68	      name: source.name,
    69	      floor,
    70	      requested: source.actualSize,
    71	      granted,
    72	      dropped: Math.max(0, source.actualSize - granted),
    73	    });
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  // Step 2: Redistribute overflow by priority
    77	  if (overflowPool > 0) {
    78	    for (const priorityName of PRIORITY_ORDER) {
    79	      const alloc = allocations.find(a => a.name === priorityName);
    80	      if (!alloc) continue;
    81	
    82	      const headroom = alloc.requested - alloc.granted;
    83	      if (headroom <= 0) continue;
    84	
    85	      const bonus = Math.min(headroom, overflowPool);
    86	      alloc.granted += bonus;
    87	      alloc.dropped -= bonus;
    88	      overflowPool -= bonus;
    89	
    90	      if (overflowPool <= 0) break;
    91	    }
    92	  }
    93	
    94	  // Step 3: Enforce total budget cap (trim in reverse priority order)
    95	  let totalUsed = allocations.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.granted, 0);
    96	  if (totalUsed > totalBudget) {
    97	    const reversed = [...PRIORITY_ORDER].reverse();
    98	    for (const name of reversed) {
    99	      if (totalUsed <= totalBudget) break;
   100	      const alloc = allocations.find(a => a.name === name);
   101	      if (!alloc) continue;
   102	
   103	      const excess = totalUsed - totalBudget;
   104	      const trim = Math.min(excess, alloc.granted);
   105	      alloc.granted -= trim;
   106	      alloc.dropped += trim;
   107	      totalUsed -= trim;
   108	    }
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  return {
   112	    totalBudget,
   113	    totalUsed: allocations.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.granted, 0),
   114	    overflow: overflowPool,
   115	    allocations,
   116	  };
   117	}

   120	export function createDefaultSources(

    61	    return 'error';

    65	function estimateTextTokens(text: string): number {
    66	  return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
    67	}
    68	
    69	function truncateTextToTokenBudget(text: string, maxTokens: number): string {
    70	  if (maxTokens <= 0) {
    71	    return '';
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  if (estimateTextTokens(text) <= maxTokens) {
    75	    return text;
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  const maxChars = Math.max(0, (maxTokens * 4) - 3);
    79	  return `${text.slice(0, maxChars).trimEnd()}...`;
    80	}

    82	function estimateStructuralContractTokens(
    83	  summary: string,
    84	  highlights: string[] | undefined,
    85	  recommendedAction: string,
    86	): number {
    87	  return estimateTextTokens([
    88	    summary,
    89	    ...(highlights ?? []),
    90	    recommendedAction,
    91	  ].join('\n'));
    92	}

    95	  summary: string,
    96	  highlights: string[] | undefined,
    97	  recommendedAction: string,
    98	): {
    99	  summary: string;
   100	  highlights: string[] | undefined;
   101	  recommendedAction: string;
   102	} {
   103	  let fittedSummary = summary;
   104	  let fittedHighlights = highlights ? [...highlights] : undefined;
   105	  let fittedRecommendedAction = recommendedAction;
   106	
   107	  while (fittedHighlights && fittedHighlights.length > 0
   108	    && estimateStructuralContractTokens(fittedSummary, fittedHighlights, fittedRecommendedAction) > STRUCTURAL_CONTRACT_MAX_TOKENS) {
   109	    fittedHighlights = fittedHighlights.slice(0, -1);
   110	  }
   111	
   112	  if (estimateStructuralContractTokens(fittedSummary, fittedHighlights, fittedRecommendedAction) > STRUCTURAL_CONTRACT_MAX_TOKENS) {
   113	    const reservedTokens = estimateStructuralContractTokens('', fittedHighlights, fittedRecommendedAction);
   114	    const summaryBudget = Math.max(40, STRUCTURAL_CONTRACT_MAX_TOKENS - reservedTokens);
   115	    fittedSummary = truncateTextToTokenBudget(fittedSummary, summaryBudget);

   593	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   594	// 6. TOKEN BUDGET ESTIMATION
   595	
   596	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   597	/**
   598	 * Provides the estimateTokens helper.
   599	 */
   600	export function estimateTokens(content: string | unknown): number {
   601	  if (!content) return 0;
   602	  const text = typeof content === 'string' ? content : JSON.stringify(content);
   603	  return Math.max(1, Math.ceil(text.length / PREFLIGHT_CONFIG.charsPerToken));
   604	}
   605	
   606	/**
   607	 * Provides the checkTokenBudget helper.
   608	 */
   609	export function checkTokenBudget(content: string, options: {
   610	  maxTokens?: number;
   611	  warning_threshold?: number;
   612	  include_embedding_overhead?: boolean;
   613	} = {}): TokenBudgetResult {
   614	  const {
   615	    maxTokens = PREFLIGHT_CONFIG.max_tokens_per_memory,
   616	    warning_threshold = PREFLIGHT_CONFIG.warning_threshold,
   617	    include_embedding_overhead = true,
   618	  } = options;
   619	
   620	  const result: TokenBudgetResult = {
   621	    within_budget: true,
   622	    estimated_tokens: 0,
   623	    maxTokens,
   624	    percentage_used: 0,
   625	    warnings: [],
   626	    errors: [],
   627	  };
   628	
   629	  if (!content) {
   630	    result.warnings.push('No content provided for token budget check');
   631	    return result;
   632	  }
   633	
   634	  // Estimate tokens for content
   635	  let estimated = estimateTokens(content);
   636	
   637	  // Add overhead for embedding API call (context + response)
   638	  if (include_embedding_overhead) {
   639	    const embeddingOverhead = 150;
   640	    estimated += embeddingOverhead;
   641	  }
   642	
   643	  result.estimated_tokens = estimated;
   644	  result.percentage_used = estimated / maxTokens;
   645	
   646	  // Check if over budget
   647	  if (estimated > maxTokens) {
   648	    result.within_budget = false;
   649	    result.errors.push({
   650	      code: PreflightErrorCodes.TOKEN_BUDGET_EXCEEDED,
   651	      message: `Content exceeds token budget: ${estimated} tokens (max: ${maxTokens})`,
   652	      suggestion: `Reduce content by approximately ${estimated - maxTokens} tokens (${Math.ceil((estimated - maxTokens) * PREFLIGHT_CONFIG.charsPerToken)} characters)`,
   653	    });
   654	  }
   655	  // Check if approaching budget
   656	  else if (result.percentage_used >= warning_threshold) {
   657	    result.warnings.push({
   658	      code: PreflightErrorCodes.TOKEN_BUDGET_WARNING,
   659	      message: `Content is ${Math.round(result.percentage_used * 100)}% of token budget (${estimated}/${maxTokens} tokens)`,
   660	      suggestion: 'Consider splitting into smaller memories for better retrieval',
   661	    });
   662	  }
   663	
   664	  return result;
   665	}

   432	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   433	   2. TOKEN BUDGET ENFORCEMENT (T205)
   434	   
   435	   Enforces per-layer/per-mode token budgets by estimating the
   436	   token count of strategy results and truncating when exceeded.
   437	   Uses character-based estimation: 1 token ≈ 4 chars.
   438	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   439	
   440	/**
   441	 * T205: Enforce token budget on strategy results.
   442	 * 
   443	 * Estimates the token count of the serialized result. If over budget,
   444	 * parses embedded result arrays and removes lowest-priority items
   445	 * until within budget. Higher-scored results are preserved.
   446	 */
   447	function enforceTokenBudget(result: ContextResult, budgetTokens: number): { result: ContextResult; enforcement: TokenBudgetEnforcement } {
   448	  const serialized = JSON.stringify(result);
   449	  const actualTokens = estimateTokens(serialized);
   450	
   451	  // Under budget — no enforcement needed
   452	  if (actualTokens <= budgetTokens) {
   453	    return {
   454	      result,
   455	      enforcement: {
   456	        budgetTokens,
   457	        actualTokens,
   458	        enforced: false,
   459	        truncated: false,
   460	      }
   461	    };
   462	  }
   463	
   464	  // REQ-002 (Cluster 1) Sanity guard: when reported usage is far below budget but
   465	  // we somehow entered enforcement (e.g. estimator ran twice on already-truncated
   466	  // payload, or budget was passed in as a tiny number), short-circuit and return
   467	  // the unmodified result. This prevents the historical regression where a
   468	  // 71-token payload against a 3000-token budget was nuked to count:0,results:[].
   469	  if (budgetTokens > 0 && actualTokens / budgetTokens < 0.50) {
   470	    return {
   471	      result,
   472	      enforcement: {
   473	        budgetTokens,
   474	        actualTokens,
   475	        enforced: false,
   476	        truncated: false,
   477	      }
   478	    };
   479	  }
   480	
   481	  // Over budget — attempt to truncate embedded results
   482	  // Strategy results contain an embedded MCPResponse with content[0].text as JSON
   483	  // That JSON has a .data.results array we can truncate
   484	  const truncatedResult = { ...result };
   485	  let parseFailed = false;
   486	  let originalResultCount: number | undefined;
   487	  let returnedResultCount: number | undefined;
   488	
   489	  const fallbackToStructuredBudget = (
   490	    baseResult: ContextResult,
   491	    parseFailedInnerText?: string,
   492	    preservedResults?: Array<Record<string, unknown>>,
   493	  ): ContextResult => {
   494	    const fallbackResult = { ...baseResult } as ContextResult;
   495	    const fallbackContent = Array.isArray((fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content)
   496	      ? ((fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<Record<string, unknown>>)
   497	      : [];
   498	    const contentClone = fallbackContent.map((entry) => ({ ...entry }));
   499	
   500	    // REQ-002 (Cluster 1): When structural truncation already produced a non-empty
   501	    // result set, preserve it rather than silently dropping to count:0,results:[].
   502	    // The previous behaviour caused the wrapper to report `returnedResultCount > 0`
   503	    // in metadata while shipping an empty payload to the caller.
   504	    const preservedSafe: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = Array.isArray(preservedResults)
   505	      ? preservedResults
   506	      : [];
   507	
   508	    const buildPreservedCandidates = (): Array<Record<string, unknown>> => {
   509	      if (preservedSafe.length === 0) {
   510	        return [];
   511	      }
   512	      const minimalResults = preservedSafe.map((r) => ({
   513	        id: r.id,
   514	        title: r.title,
   515	        similarity: r.similarity,
   516	        specFolder: r.specFolder,
   517	        confidence: r.confidence,
   518	        importanceTier: r.importanceTier,
   519	        isConstitutional: r.isConstitutional,
   520	        metadataOnly: true,
   521	      }));
   522	      return [
   523	        {
   524	          summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   525	          data: {
   526	            count: preservedSafe.length,
   527	            results: preservedSafe,
   528	          },
   529	          meta: {
   530	            tool: 'memory_search',
   531	            truncated: true,
   532	            preserved: true,
   533	          },
   534	        },
   535	        {
   536	          summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   537	          data: {
   538	            count: minimalResults.length,
   539	            results: minimalResults,
   540	          },
   541	          meta: {
   542	            tool: 'memory_search',
   543	            truncated: true,
   544	            preserved: true,
   545	            metadataOnly: true,
   546	          },
   547	        },
   548	      ];
   549	    };
   550	
   551	    const emptyCandidates: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = [
   552	      {
   553	        summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   554	        data: {
   555	          count: 0,
   556	          results: [],
   557	        },
   558	        meta: {
   559	          tool: 'memory_search',
   560	          truncated: true,

The main truncation function is [enforceTokenBudget](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts:447). It enforces `memory_context` budgets by truncating content fields, dropping lowest-scored results, adding metadata-only fallbacks, then falling back to compact structured output.

The file explicitly says advisory-only; enforcement happens downstream.
